Cute little shop tucked into a corner and wow this place is great for a cute date! Came with no wait on a Saturday night and this place has a really great wait staff who constantly checked in with me and even gave me a napkin when I spilled something and didn‚Äôt realize he noticed.

Standout dishes were the paratha for sure it was some of the most soft and flavorful paratha I‚Äôve ever had and it goes great with the curry sauce.

The coconut chicken noodle soup was great too with the soft chewy noodles and yummy soup base. The moneybags weren‚Äôt as yummy  but we‚Äôre super chewy and unique.< /review>

<Text>The menu is full of great choices. For vegetarians, vegans, and gluten-free needs, they've got you covered, with most of the menu being vegetarian from the start, with well-marked vegan and gluten free items.

We started with one of the chaats, and it was a lovely way to start the meal. The fried potato cakes and seasoned chickpeas were tasty and not too heavy.

The eggplant dosa and palak paneer dosa were perfect. The eggplant (baigan bharta) was seasoned in a way I hadn't had before, full of cardamom and bright flavors of onion. The palak paneer had great and plentiful pieces of cheese, with a spinach sauce that was just the right balance between earthy and lively.

Our server was helpful and friendly, as well as the waiter that refilled our water. The grocery had many items that I'd like to come back and pick up.< /Text>< rate>
5< /rate>

I was excited for a nice dinner and drinks with my husband and my father. We are making sure to support our local restaurants and businesses so Powells was on our list.
I'll start with the good! The bartender was their saving grace and he is the ONLY reason they get any stars at all! We were able to enjoy a cold beer because the bartender took and provided our drink order while we were on our way out back to our seats. Unfortunately, we did not eat. We were never even offered a menu! Our group of 3 was seated for more than 30 minutes and the waitress never even greeted us! Not only that, but she never offered water, drinks, a menu, much less a "hello"
Trying to make the best of a bad start we pulled the menu up online. We decided to make our selections so we could place an order when the opportunity presented itself. We assumed said opportunity wouldn't be too terribly far away because there was only 3 other seated groups (1 out front and 2 out back) so we should be acknowledged relatively quick. NOPE! Boy were we wrong! It was almost 40 minutes before we finally decided it was time to leave! We chose not to give up on our night so we walked across the street to another restaurant.
We enjoyed wonderful service, food, and drinks at Cascada!<//text>

They serve their beer in mason jars (even their tasters) so they are hip as well. <rating>5</rating><user>116960664827592173728<//user><Date>1570504700244</Date><Gmap_id>0x809b052c5f021b37:0x996879fb6d3229d6<//Gmap_id></record>

<response>None</response>< Review>
We were sure people had been paid to write such great reviews for the newly named Burger and Cream; clearly after experiencing them post Foster's, we were wrong. Their burgers are FAR superior to any I've ever had at a Foster's Freeze - probably thanks to the Truckee Sourdough Co. bread, fresh high quality produce, meats and cheeses. They still carry crinkle cut fries - a huge plus for me as I always counted on Foster's having them.  Customer service has greatly improved as well.
One thing I will say can be improved is the vanilla soft serve. What they have now is still decent, but it doesn't have the crave-ability that the vanilla soft serve had previously.

{Burger and Cream} is definitely worth a try!  Give them a go and see if you agree.</Review>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Found this place by accident while passing through the area and stopped for lunch. Steady stream of people seemed to be regulars. There is some inside seating, but we (like many other customers) ordered at the window and ate outside. Limited outdoor seating, but the turnover was relatively quick. Outdoor-access bathrooms were well-maintained. Great burger (fresh, tender, well-proportioned [not all bread]) and exceptional desserts, including a Chocolatey Peanut Butter Banana Twist that knocked my socks off. I guess the place used to be a Foster's Freeze franchise, but they parted ways with the parent company in order to better serve their customers, and it's remained a family-owned and operated business for several decades. I'll definitely go out of my way to eat there again.< /Review>
